PlanPrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment. 
* For each action, use the formatting as specified in Valid Actions.
* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `reverse_search`
   * Description: Performs a reverse image search to find similar images on the web.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will perform a reverse search to find similar images.
   * Format: reverse_search(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

# Example: reverse_search()

```
reverse_search(<image:k>)
```

JudgePrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `not enough information`: The fact-check does not contain sufficient information to come to an conclusion. For example,there is substantial lack of evidence or the evidence is inconclusive, conflicting or self-contradictory. In the case of a lack of evidence, state which information exactly is missing. In particular, if no RESULTS or sources are available, pick this decision.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment. 
* For each action, use the formatting as specified in Valid Actions.
* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `reverse_search`
   * Description: Performs a reverse image search to find similar images on the web.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will perform a reverse search to find similar images.
   * Format: reverse_search(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

### [California Wildfires](https://www.npr.org/series/g-s1-41621/california-wildfires)

"It is the latest in a long string of assertions by Russian officials, media, and the pro-Kremlin online ecosystem that Ukrainian officials are corrupt and use foreign aid money to enrich themselves." L√©a Ronzaud, a senior investigator at research firm Graphika, told NPR in an email.

[!Russian navy recruits perform with the Russian flag in St. <image:2336>](https://www.npr.org/2024/06/06/g-s1-2965/russia-propaganda-deepfakes-sham-websites-social-media-ukraine)

### [Untangling Disinformation](https://www.npr.org/series/973275370/untangling-disinformation)

### [This is what Russian propaganda looks like in 2024](https://www.npr.org/2024/06/06/g-s1-2965/russia-propaganda-deepfakes-sham-websites-social-media-ukraine)

"It's just so typical of what we see from Russia, \[to\] take advantage of an ongoing crisis for their own ends," said Darren Linvill, a communications professor and co-director of Clemson University's Media Forensics Hub.

The Ukrainian general story first emerged on a pro-Russian Telegram channel four days after the fires started in Los Angeles. Some of the posts amplifying the baseless claim falsely credited it to United24 Media, a website affiliated with the Ukrainian government.

The Ukrainian National Security and Defense Council's Center for Countering Disinformation issued a [statement](https://x.com/CforCD/status/1878381491056501245)
 describing the claim as "Russian propaganda." It said it had verified with United24 Media that it did not create or share the story.

NPR has not obtained evidence that any Ukrainian generals owned homes in Los Angeles that were destroyed by the fires. Both @OlgaBazova and Patterson's posts received user-generated community notes on X citing the Greek fact check.

The unverified claim about the alleged Ukrainian-owned mansions also appeared on other social media platforms including Tik Tok, TruthSocial and the Russian site VK, but did not gain much traction.

The story is the latest example of Russia's shift away from using fake social media profiles impersonating real people, as it did during the 2016 and 2020 U.S. Accounts tied to previous China influence operations spread false claims about the fire's origins.

While the story about Ukrainian officials got more traction than the other narratives about the fires originating from Russia-allied channels, Linvill said, it has not yet spread as widely as previous narratives linked to Russia."

The story was debunked by fact-checkers from Greece and the United States. <image:2335> The Ukrainian National Security and Defense Council's Center for Countering Disinformation described the claim as "Russian propaganda."

JudgePrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `not enough information`: The fact-check does not contain sufficient information to come to an conclusion. For example,there is substantial lack of evidence or the evidence is inconclusive, conflicting or self-contradictory. In the case of a lack of evidence, state which information exactly is missing. In particular, if no RESULTS or sources are available, pick this decision.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.

_In order to analyse all of these tweets, we used a method created by researchers in cognitive science at the French higher education institute l__'√â__cole Normale sup√©rieure (for more on the method click_¬†[_here_](https://www.frontiersin.org/journals/artificial-intelligence/articles/10.3389/frai.2024.1365508/full)
_), which allowed us to catagorise text using the ChatGPT language model._

_We asked ChatGPT‚Äôs API to categorise each tweet, which enabled us to identify all of the tweets that Musk shared that were either hostile to Ukraine or favorable to Russia, as well as those that criticised Europe and those that showed support for the European far right._¬†

_We verified the results by manually analysing each post._¬†¬†

_We examined Musk‚Äôs original posts, as well as the posts he shared (such as his retweets or quote tweets). We also included the transcripts of videos that he posted directly or shared from other accounts._

([https://collegeofems.com/Coin-Display-Wall-Hanging-Coin-Collecting-Holders-Dollar-Bill/983708](https://collegeofems.com/Coin-Display-Wall-Hanging-Coin-Collecting-Holders-Dollar-Bill/983708)), which is not available. The same image was found on Etsy ([https://www.etsy.com/ie/listing/1407539034/custom-dollar-dollar-bill-art-100-dollar](https://www.etsy.com/ie/listing/1407539034/custom-dollar-dollar-bill-art-100-dollar)) as a custom dollar bill art. The image was also found on Redbubble ([https://www.redbubble.com/shop/one+dollar+stickers](https://www.redbubble.com/shop/one+dollar+stickers)) as a sticker. <image:2384>, <image:2385>, <image:2386>, <image:2387>, <image:2388>, <image:2389>, <image:2390>, <image:2391>, <image:2392>, <image:2393>, <image:2394>, <image:2405>, <image:19>


## Elaboration
The claim is false. The AOL article states that the image is fake. The reverse image search shows that the image is a custom dollar bill art and a sticker.


## Final Judgement
The image is a custom dollar bill art and a sticker, and the AOL article states that the image is fake. Therefore, the claim is not factually accurate. `false`

## Summary



===== > RESPONSE:  < =====
The claim is false. The image of the tweet is a custom dollar bill art and a sticker, and an article from AOL ([https://www.aol.com/fact-check-elon-musk-didn-164103080.html](https://www.aol.com/fact-check-elon-musk-didn-164103080.html)) states that the image is fake.

* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `reverse_search`
   * Description: Performs a reverse image search to find similar images on the web.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will perform a reverse search to find similar images.
   * Format: reverse_search(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

## Decision Options
* `not enough information`: The fact-check does not contain sufficient information to come to an conclusion. For example,there is substantial lack of evidence or the evidence is inconclusive, conflicting or self-contradictory. In the case of a lack of evidence, state which information exactly is missing. In particular, if no RESULTS or sources are available, pick this decision.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment.

## Valid Actions
* `reverse_search`
   * Description: Performs a reverse image search to find similar images on the web.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will perform a reverse search to find similar images.
   * Format: reverse_search(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

Vice President JD Vance warned on Thursday that the United States could hit Russia with economic and military ‚Äútools of leverage‚Äù if Russian leader Vladimir Putin doesn‚Äôt negotiate a peace deal with Ukraine in good faith.

Speaking to the Wall Street Journal on Thursday, Vance said the option of sending US troops to Ukraine was ‚Äúon the table,‚Äù as well as economic punishment if a peace deal doesn‚Äôt guarantee Kyiv‚Äôs long-term independence.

‚ÄúThere are economic tools of leverage, there are of course military tools of leverage,‚Äù Vance told the newspaper.

His comments strike a different tone from other recent statements from the White House ‚Äì including from US President Donald Trump who [suggested this week](https://www.cnn.com/2025/02/11/europe/ukraine-russia-trump-zelensky-intl/index.html)

‚ÄúEurope is of course a very important ally to the United States, NATO is a very important military alliance ‚Ä¶ but we want to make sure NATO is actually built for the future, and part of that is ensuring that NATO does a little bit more burden-sharing in Europe so the United States can focus on some of our challenges in East Asia,‚Äù Vance said, speaking to reporters beside NATO Secretary General Mark Rutte.

JudgePrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `not enough information`: The fact-check does not contain sufficient information to come to an conclusion. For example,there is substantial lack of evidence or the evidence is inconclusive, conflicting or self-contradictory. In the case of a lack of evidence, state which information exactly is missing. In particular, if no RESULTS or sources are available, pick this decision.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment.

* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `reverse_search`
   * Description: Performs a reverse image search to find similar images on the web.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will perform a reverse search to find similar images.
   * Format: reverse_search(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

### TEHRAN (Tasnim) - Russian Foreign Ministry Spokeswoman Maria Zakharova commented on reports that hundreds of prisoners have been mobilized to extinguish fires in the US state of California, pointing to the hypocrisy of the US.

[\- Other Media news -](/en/service/1200/other-media)

The diplomat noted that in 2023, Washington restricted imports of products from several Chinese companies in an attempt to exclude goods allegedly produced with the help of Uygur forced labor from the US supply chain.

"This raises a logical question: will Congress draft a bill imposing sanctions on California authorities, private companies, and ordinary Americans for using prison labor to put out fires?" she wondered. "We are so sick of this hypocrisy!" Zakharova added.

Wildfires began to spread across Los Angeles County on January 7."

Assessing Claims That Russia Offered Sanctuary to California Fire Victims
=========================================================================

One Russian governor did make an offer, but there are some caveats.

! A single Russian governor said that he would welcome California fire victims to the region of occupied Ukraine he oversees, but only if they don‚Äôt support the government in Kyiv.

On Monday, Vladimir Saldo, the governor of the Russian-occupied Kherson oblast region of Ukraine, [told](https://tass.ru/obschestvo/22867057)
 _TASS_‚Äîa Russian state-controlled media outlet‚Äîthat the region would accept any Americans who lost their homes in this month‚Äôs California fires. ‚ÄúDespite the ongoing, blatantly anti-Russian policy of the United States, we fully understand that natural disasters don‚Äôt care who you are or what you do,‚Äù Saldo said, [according to](https://www.rt.com/russia/610836-california-fires-sanctuary-kherson/)
 Russia Today, a Russian state-controlled network that translated the statement into English. Therefore, our region is ready to welcome any American citizen who has lost their home and livelihood.‚Äù

That offer comes with a caveat, applying only to Californians who haven‚Äôt supported Ukraine since Russia invaded its borders in February 2022. Sutton")
, and [Cole Murphy](https://thedispatch.com/author/cole-murphy/ "Posts by Cole Murphy")

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `not enough information`: The fact-check does not contain sufficient information to come to an conclusion. For example,there is substantial lack of evidence or the evidence is inconclusive, conflicting or self-contradictory. In the case of a lack of evidence, state which information exactly is missing. In particular, if no RESULTS or sources are available, pick this decision.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.

## Valid Actions
* `reverse_search`
   * Description: Performs a reverse image search to find similar images on the web.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will perform a reverse search to find similar images.
   * Format: reverse_search(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

Inflaming Divides: Russian Narratives on the California Wildfires
=================================================================

January 15, 2025

[![Krysia](/sites/default/files/styles/headshot_thumbnail/public/2023-12/33.png?itok=AqrjfUeB)](/find-experts/krystyna-sikora "Krystyna Sikora")

by

[Krystyna Sikora](/find-experts/krystyna-sikora "Krystyna Sikora")

3 min read

[Share](# "share")

[Artificial Intelligence](/news?sort_bef_combine=field_date_value_DESC&topics%5B254%5D=254)

[Authoritarian Interference](/news?sort_bef_combine=field_date_value_DESC&topics%5B49%5D=49)

[Domestic Politics and Society](/news?sort_bef_combine=field_date_value_DESC&topics%5B60%5D=60)

[Russia](/news?sort_bef_combine=field_date_value_DESC&region%5B32%5D=32)

[United States](/news?sort_bef_combine=field_date_value_DESC&region%5B29%5D=29)

[Print Article](/download/article/23979)

Last week, devastating wildfires ignited across Los Angeles County in what is one of the most destructive natural disasters in US history. But as firefighters continue to battle the flames, false¬†and misleading information about the disaster¬†[has spread](https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2025/jan/10/rightwing-misinformation-los-angeles-fire)
¬†just as quickly on social media.¬†While¬†much¬†of the¬†false¬†information¬†seemingly¬†originated¬†from users in the United States, Russian¬†state-affiliated accounts also¬†leveraged¬†the California wildfires¬†and narratives reverberating among certain segments of the US public¬†to¬†sow division, undermine trust in relief efforts, and reduce public support for Ukraine.¬†¬†

**Diverting¬†Resources to Ukraine**¬†

Amid the destructive wildfires in Los Angeles, Russian government officials and state-affiliated media have propagated narratives critical of the Biden administration and other Democratic leaders to aggravate political division, particularly on Ukraine, and to denigrate the United States. Russian-state controlled outlet Sputnik further¬†[mocked](https://x.com/Sputnik_India/status/1879127371049001320)
¬†Biden‚Äôs emergency relief payments to victims of the wildfires, claiming that they receive less daily per capita than people in Ukraine and Israel.¬†¬†

Russian state-controlled media outlets further¬†[honed in](https://sputnikglobe.com/20250109/california-wildfires-unexpected-links-to-us-green-lobby-and-ukraine-1121391704.html)
¬†[on reports](https://x.com/SputnikInt/status/1877282105815597399)
¬†that the Los Angeles Fire Department (LAFD) donated surplus equipment to Ukraine in 2022¬†[to suggest](https://x.com/SputnikInt/status/1877345987468882396)
¬†that those donations¬†[created a lack of](https://x.com/RT_com/status/1877126472915128820)
¬†resources to fight fires. Additionally, Russian state media seized on the fires to fuel divides on other partisan policy issues, linking the fires to the ‚Äú[green lobby](https://sputnikglobe.com/20250109/california-wildfires-unexpected-links-to-us-green-lobby-and-ukraine-1121391704.html)
‚Äù and¬†[blaming](https://x.com/RT_com/status/1877151147703562608)
¬†the firefighter shortage on COVID-19 vaccine mandates.

**Amplifying**¬†**AI-Generated Content**

In at least one case, Russian state media amplified a misleading image generated by artificial intelligence (AI). Other Russian-language media outlets subsequently spread the image.¬†

**Conclusion**¬†

Kremlin-affiliated accounts have leveraged the California wildfires to further advance Russia‚Äôs geopolitical agenda. In a press conference on January 14, Russian Foreign Minister Sergey Lavrov¬†[claimed](https://x.com/SputnikInt/status/1879100711361016212)
¬†the estimated $250 billion worth of damage sustained from the California fires is comparable to the amount Washington ‚Äúpumped into Ukraine‚Äù. Russia‚Äôs messaging on the wildfires further underlines a trend of autocratic states¬†[exploiting natural disasters](https://www.nbcnews.com/news/investigations/russia-china-cuba-amplified-falsehoods-recent-hurricanes-us-official-s-rcna177672)
¬†to advance their geopolitical goals. This approach keeps with Russia‚Äôs now¬†[longstanding strategy](https://securingdemocracy.gmfus.org/a-year-of-disinformation-russia-and-chinas-influence-campaigns-during-the-war-in-ukraine/)
¬†to dent US support for Ukraine by playing to pocketbook issues and perceptions that domestic issues have received less attention than foreign ones.¬†

![](/sites/default/files/inline-images/rt%201.png)

**Blaming DEI**

Accounts affiliated with Russia echoed narratives prominent among American audiences that claim diversity, equity, and inclusion (DEI) initiatives hindered wildfire recovery efforts. Russian state-controlled media outlet RT¬†[accused](https://x.com/RT_com/status/1876870822637248582)
¬†LAFD Chief Kristen Crowly‚Äîthe first woman and openly gay person to serve in the role‚Äîof prioritizing DEI initiatives at the expense of preventing fires. Sputnik also¬†[posted](https://x.com/SputnikInt/status/1877278684240859332)
¬†a local news clip of a California resident who claimed that ‚Äúgay people‚Äù were the cause of the fires."

The article also mentions that Russian accounts echoed narratives that DEI initiatives hindered wildfire recovery efforts. <image:1>

MARY LOUISE KELLY, HOST:

And now to California, where firefighters in Los Angeles are making progress getting those massive wildfires under control. Now, NPR has learned that Russia is using the fires to advance anti-Ukraine propaganda as part of its war against that country. So far, there's no evidence that it happened, and the Ukrainian government has denied it to NPR, but researchers say that it is part of a bigger narrative that Russia has pushed for years. Pro-Russian accounts regularly claim that various Ukrainian officials own luxury goods overseas, like yachts, villas and, in one case, a sports car. The underlying idea is that Ukrainian government is corrupt and does not deserve foreign aid, which it is currently receiving for its war with Russia. How did it spread?

HUO: So fact-checkers traced this narrative to pro-Russian Telegram channels. A lot of these accounts and websites have a history of either being a part of or echoing known Russian-influenced operations. Darren Linvill is a professor at Clemson University and codirects its media forensics lab.

DARREN LINVILL: It's just so typical of what we see from Russia and so despicable to take advantage of an ongoing crisis for their own ends.

HUO: You know, aside from undermining Ukraine, Russia also wants to sow internal discord in the United States. We see this both in this disaster and in the Maui fires in 2023.

KELLY: Yeah.

HUO: Russian state media amplified American - often conservative - voices criticizing the government's disaster response. This didn't get much traction, though.

KELLY: And this specific false claim - has it gotten much traction - traveled very far?

HUO: So it's gotten a million views on X with help from one pro-Russian influencer and then an American influencer."

The Ukrainian general story first emerged on a pro-Russian Telegram channel four days after the fires started in Los Angeles. Within hours, it was amplified by several other sources, including another Telegram channel which labeled it as satire, an X account, and a website that resembles a [pro-Russian network](https://www.sgdsn.gouv.fr/files/files/20240212_NP_SGDSN_VIGINUM_PORTAL-KOMBAT-NETWORK_ENG_VF.pdf)

JudgePrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `not enough information`: The fact-check does not contain sufficient information to come to an conclusion. For example,there is substantial lack of evidence or the evidence is inconclusive, conflicting or self-contradictory. In the case of a lack of evidence, state which information exactly is missing. In particular, if no RESULTS or sources are available, pick this decision.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.

PlanPrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment. 
* For each action, use the formatting as specified in Valid Actions.
* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `reverse_search`
   * Description: Performs a reverse image search to find similar images on the web.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will perform a reverse search to find similar images.
   * Format: reverse_search(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

# Record
## Claim
Claim: "Russia offered assistance for the California wildfires from January 2025."

## Actions
```
web_search("Russia California wildfires assistance 2025")
```

## Evidence
### Evidence from `web_search`
Tasnim News Agency published an article on January 12, 2025, discussing Russia's comments on the California wildfires, including comments from Maria Zakharova (<image:4830>) and the spread of wildfires in Los Angeles County (<image:4831>). The Dispatch published an article on January 15, 2025, stating that Vladimir Saldo offered sanctuary to California fire victims (<image:4838>).

NPR published an article on January 16, 2025, discussing how pro-Kremlin social media accounts spread a false narrative about the Los Angeles wildfires (<image:4849>, <image:4853>).

*   [https://www.tasnimnews.com/en/news/2025/01/12/3236714/russia-notes-us-hypocrisy-in-california-fire-case](https://www.tasnimnews.com/en/news/2025/01/12/3236714/russia-notes-us-hypocrisy-in-california-fire-case)
*   [https://thedispatch.com/article/assessing-claims-that-russia-offered-sanctuary-to-california-fire-victims/](https://thedispatch.com/article/assessing-claims-that-russia-offered-sanctuary-to-california-fire-victims/)
*   [https://www.npr.org/2025/01/16/nx-s1-5259842/los-angeles-california-fires-russia-ukraine](https://www.npr.org/2025/01/16/nx-s1-5259842/los-angeles-california-fires-russia-ukraine)


## Elaboration
The evidence indicates that Russia commented on the California wildfires in January 2025. Maria Zakharova made comments, and Vladimir Saldo offered sanctuary to fire victims. However, the evidence does not explicitly state that Russia offered assistance for the wildfires. The NPR article mentions that pro-Kremlin social media accounts spread a false narrative about the wildfires.

Therefore, the claim is not directly supported by the evidence. The evidence suggests that Russia was involved in the discussion and offered sanctuary, but not assistance.

To verify the claim, information about any specific offers of assistance from Russia is missing.


## Actions
```
web_search("Russia assistance California wildfires")
```

## Evidence
### Evidence from `web_search`
The German Marshall Fund published an article on January 15, 2025, discussing how Russian state-affiliated accounts leveraged the California wildfires to sow division and undermine trust in relief efforts, and reduce public support for Ukraine (<image:1>). NPR and OPB published articles on January 16, 2025, discussing how Russia used the California wildfires to advance anti-Ukraine propaganda, with pro-Kremlin social media accounts spreading false narratives. The OPB article mentions that the story was debunked by fact-checkers.

*   [https://www.gmfus.org/news/inflaming-divides-russian-narratives-california-wildfires](https://www.gmfus.org/news/inflaming-divides-russian-narratives-california-wildfires)
*   [https://www.npr.org/transcripts/nx-s1-5259842](https://www.npr.org/transcripts/nx-s1-5259842)
*   [https://www.opb.org/article/2025/01/16/russia-tries-to-use-california-fires-to-discredit-ukraine/](https://www.opb.org/article/2025/01/16/russia-tries-to-use-california-fires-to-discredit-ukraine/)


## Elaboration
The new evidence reinforces the previous findings. It highlights that Russia leveraged the California wildfires to sow division and spread anti-Ukraine propaganda. However, the evidence still does not mention any offers of assistance from Russia.

Therefore, the claim remains unverified. The evidence focuses on Russia's use of the wildfires for propaganda purposes, not on providing aid.

Russia exploits wildfires in Los Angeles to push anti-US, anti-Ukraine propaganda
=================================================================================

January 16, 2025 8:15 AM

*   By [Leonid Martynyuk](/author/leonid-martynyuk/oymt_ "Leonid Martynyuk")
    

* * *

!Fire crews battle the Kenneth Fire in the West Hills section of Los Angeles, California, Jan. 9, 2025.

¬†[](https://www.voanews.com)

Russia exploits wildfires in Los Angeles to push anti-US, anti-Ukraine propaganda

#### Maria Zakharova

Russian Foreign Ministry spokeswoman

U.S. uses forced labor by involving inmates in fighting Los Angeles fires, while sanctioning China for using forced labor in Xinjiang.

[Source: RIA Novosti, January 12, 2025](https://ria.ru/20250112/zaharova-1993301092.html "Source: RIA Novosti, January 12, 2025")

False

Russian foreign ministry spokeswoman Maria Zakharova accused the United States of ‚Äúobscurantist hypocrisy‚Äù for allowing inmates to fight Los Angeles wildfires. has been condemning for years.

"Hundreds of prisoners have been recruited to fight wildfires in southern California ‚Ä¶ In recent years, U.S. officials have repeatedly criticized China for using forced labor, especially in the Xinjiang Uyghur Autonomous Region ‚Ä¶ \[W\]ill Congress impose sanctions on the California government, private companies, and ordinary Americans for using prison labor to fight fires."

The claim is false.

[In California, inmates voluntarily join firefighting crews](https://www.npr.org/2025/01/10/nx-s1-5254122/inmate-firefighters-california-wildfires)
 if they meet the program‚Äôs qualifications, which consider physical fitness and behavioral records. government is impoverishing its own citizens.

Speaking at a January 14 press conference on the results of Russian diplomacy in 2024, Lavrov said, that Americans ‚Äúburned almost all of California,‚Äù and the damage is estimated $250 billion, which is ‚Äúcomparable‚Äù to what the U.S. pledged to [Ukraine](https://www.state.gov/bureau-of-political-military-affairs/releases/2025/01/u-s-security-cooperation-with-ukraine)
 about $66.2 billion in [security assistance](https://media.defense.gov/2025/Jan/09/2003626079/-1/-1/1/KEY-ACHIEVEMENTS-AND-FACTS-US-SECURITY-ASSISTANCE-TO-UKRAINE.PDF)
 between 2014, when Russia annexed Crimea, and February 2022 when Moscow launched a war, and about $66.5 billion since.

Lavrov‚Äôs claim that by aiding Ukraine the U.S. society, in part due to the [Russian propaganda influence](https://www.npr.org/2024/09/07/nx-s1-5101895/doj-says-russia-paid-right-wing-influencers-to-spread-russian-propaganda)
.

Experts, however, argue that opposite to draining American economy, the large portion of the Ukraine aid is being reinvested domestically, [boosting defense manufacturing industry and sustaining jobs](https://www.wilsoncenter.org/blog-post/us-aid-ukraine-helps-american-economy-and-boosts-us-jobs)
.

Russian propaganda exploited the Ukrainian angle in the Los Angeles fires trying to spread false accusations against Ukraine‚Äôs military command of misappropriating the Western aid.

Russia‚Äôs newly emerged group of social media influencers nicknamed ‚Äúmilbloggers‚Äù as most members are either Russian combatants or pro-war reporters from the battle lines in Ukraine, played key role in creating and spreading such false claims.

Russian Telegram channel Voennyj obozrevatel' (Military Observer) alleged on January 11, that eight mansions worth a total of $90 million owned by high-ranking Ukrainian military officials, were destroyed in the Los Angeles wildfires.

‚ÄúAccording to Ukrainian sources, 8 mansions owned by high-ranking Ukrainian military personnel were burned during large-scale wildfires in Los Angeles. The total value of these properties amounts to $90 million and was allegedly purchased with funds provided by the West as part of economic aid to Kyiv after the war began.‚Äù

Russian state-controlled news sites and media outlets, including Gazeta.ru, Lenta.ru, EADaily, News.ru, Komsomolskaya Pravda, Tsargrad, and Rossiyskaya Gazeta used the post in their news coverage.

[Multiple fact-checking outlets](https://www.factchecker.gr/2025/01/12/russian-propaganda-8-mansions-of-high-ranking-ukrainian-military-officials-did-not-burn-down-in-los-angeles/)
 and even some Russian news media debunked the post as lacking merit and unsubstantiated.

Yet the claim about the luxury villas of Ukrainian generals allegedly burning down in Los Angeles spread on X the following days, receiving millions of views and thousands of reposts.

In another disinformation plot, on January 13-14, Russian state-owned news sites sought to undermine President Volodymyr Zelenskyy's decision to send Ukrainian firefighters to Los Angeles to help put out the wildfires.

State-owned RIA Novosti, RT, and others used an X post by ‚ÄúUkrainian journalist‚Äù Diana Panchenko, who wrote responding to Zeleskyy‚Äôs announcement: "I am glad that hundreds of men will have the opportunity to leave Ukraine these days."

Russian news outlets generalized the post, speculating it signaled that Ukrainian journalists oppose Ukraine's fight for independence and the Ukrainian men are desperate to leave the country.

In fact, Reporters Without Borders exposed [Diana Panchenko as Russian propagandist](https://rsf.org/en/diana-panchenko-ukrainian-propagandist-working-kremlin)
 working for the Kremlin. <image:2557>

Fire crews battle the Kenneth Fire in the West Hills section of Los Angeles, California, Jan."

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.

===== > RESPONSE:  < =====
The fact-check reveals that while Russia commented on the California wildfires in January 2025 and used them for propaganda, there is no evidence from sources like Tasnim News Agency, The Dispatch, NPR, and Voice of America to support the claim that Russia offered assistance for the wildfires.

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment. 
* For each action, use the formatting as specified in Valid Actions.
* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `reverse_search`
   * Description: Performs a reverse image search to find similar images on the web.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will perform a reverse search to find similar images.
   * Format: reverse_search(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

"While American PMCs traditionally have worked closely with the US Gov and many American PMCs have interests that align with the US Gov, PMCs, irrespective of origin, are ultimately businesses," Olsen said, adding that Russia "would benefit from making up these allegations considering the stigma connected with the private military industry."

# Instructions
You just retrieved web sources, each one summarized under "Web Sources". **Your task right now is to summarize the web source summaries.**

Always adhere to the following rules:
* Write only one to two paragraphs.
* Include all URLs from the listed sources. Format them as Markdown hyperlinks.
* Do not add any additional information besides the information in the summaries.
* Include references (<image:k>) to all relevant images.

# Record
## Claim
Claim: "<image:24> This image shows American mercenaries participating in Ukraine's incursion into Russia's Kursk Oblast in August 2024."

## Actions
```
web_search("American mercenaries Ukraine Kursk Oblast August 2024")
reverse_search(<image:24>)
```

## Web Sources
**Web Search Result**

From [Source](https://www.newsweek.com/russia-protests-american-soldiers-kursk-1942273): 
Content: Newsweek reports that Russia has claimed the presence of American mercenaries in the Kursk region during Ukraine's incursion in August 2024. <image:3404>, <image:3401>, <image:3403>. The Russian Foreign Ministry expressed strong protest to the U.S. over the alleged involvement of American citizens in the incursion. The article also mentions that the U.S. has denied involvement. The article was published on August 20, 2024.


From [Source](https://www.aa.com.tr/en/russia-ukraine-war/russia-formally-protests-us-mercenaries-joining-ukrainian-soldiers-in-kursk-region-/3308755): 
Content: The Anadolu Agency published an article on August 20, 2024, stating that Russia protested the participation of US private military companies (PMCs) fighting alongside Ukraine in the Kursk region. <image:i>. The Russian Foreign Ministry claimed that US PMCs were fighting alongside Ukrainian troops in the Kursk region.


From [Source](https://www.ukrainianphotographers.com/en/news-articles/foreign-mercenaries-in-the-kursk-region): 
Content: The Ukrainian Photographers website published news stories on January 23, 2025, and January 21, 2025.


## Your Summary



===== > RESPONSE:  < =====
Newsweek reports that Russia claimed the presence of American mercenaries in the Kursk region during Ukraine's incursion in August 2024 (<image:3404>, <image:3401>, <image:3403>). The Russian Foreign Ministry protested the alleged involvement of American citizens, which the U.S. denied. The Anadolu Agency also reported on August 20, 2024, that Russia protested the participation of US private military companies fighting alongside Ukraine in the Kursk region (<image:i>).

The Ukrainian Photographers website published news stories on January 23, 2025, and January 21, 2025.

*   [Source](https://www.newsweek.com/russia-protests-american-soldiers-kursk-1942273)
*   [Source](https://www.aa.com.tr/en/russia-ukraine-war/russia-formally-protests-us-mercenaries-joining-ukrainian-soldiers-in-kursk-region-/3308755)
*   [Source](https://www.ukrainianphotographers.com/en/news-articles/foreign-mercenaries-in-the-kursk-region)

SummarizeResultPrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
In order to find evidence that helps your fact-check, you just ran a web search which yielded a Search Result. **Your task right now is to summarize the Search Result.** What to include:
* information that might be useful for the fact-check (see Record)
* relevant images (refer to images by inserting their reference <image:k>)
* if available: the release date as well as the author or the publisher (e.g. the media company) of the search result.

Do NOT include:
* advertisements
* any other information not related to the Record or the Claim

Additional rules:
* Do not add any additional information besides the information in the Search Result.
* If the Search Result doesn't contain any relevant information for the fact-checking work, simply print one word in capital letters: "NONE".
* Keep your writing style like in the Examples 1, 2 and 3 provided to you.
* Try to filter out relevant information even if the search result is in a different language.

# Example 1
The search result from America Today provides several photographs of the Notre-Dame Cathedral fire on April 15, 2019. <image:i>, <image:j>, <image:k>. None of the images show the Eiffel Tower in the background. 

# Example 2
NONE

# Example 3
The Guardian discusses a report blaming the Syrian government for a toxic gas attack and condemning their use of chemical weapons. The Guardian mentions the Chemical Weapons Convention and the responsibilities of Syria under the convention. According to The Guardian, The White House condemned the Assad regime for defying the norm against chemical weapons use.

12:06 [–ê–∫—Ç—Ä–∏—Å–∞ —Å–µ—Ä–∏–∞–ª–∞ "–•–æ–¥—è—á–∏–µ –º–µ—Ä—Ç–≤–µ—Ü—ã" –ö–µ–ª–ª–∏ –ú–∞–∫ —É–º–µ—Ä–ª–∞ –≤ –≤–æ–∑—Ä–∞—Å—Ç–µ 33 –ª–µ—Ç: —á—Ç–æ —Å—Ç–∞–ª–æ –ø—Ä–∏—á–∏–Ω–æ–π](https://apostrophe.ua/article/lime/learn/2025-08-06/aktorka-serialu-hodyachi-mertsi-kelli-mak-pomerla-u-vitsi-33-rokiv-scho-stalo-prychynoyu/62542 "–ê–º–µ—Ä–∏–∫–∞–Ω—Å–∫–∞—è –∞–∫—Ç—Ä–∏—Å–∞ –ö–µ–ª–ª–∏ –ú–∞–∫, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è —Å–Ω–∏–º–∞–ª–∞—Å—å –≤ —Å–µ—Ä–∏–∞–ª–µ "–•–æ–¥—è—á–∏–µ –º–µ—Ä—Ç–≤–µ—Ü—ã", —É–º–µ—Ä–ª–∞ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –±–æ—Ä—å–±—ã —Å —Ç—è–∂–µ–ª–æ–π –±–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω—å—é")

SummarizeResultPrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
In order to find evidence that helps your fact-check, you just ran a web search which yielded a Search Result. **Your task right now is to summarize the Search Result.** What to include:
* information that might be useful for the fact-check (see Record)
* relevant images (refer to images by inserting their reference <image:k>)
* if available: the release date as well as the author or the publisher (e.g. the media company) of the search result.

Do NOT include:
* advertisements
* any other information not related to the Record or the Claim

Additional rules:
* Do not add any additional information besides the information in the Search Result.
* If the Search Result doesn't contain any relevant information for the fact-checking work, simply print one word in capital letters: "NONE".
* Keep your writing style like in the Examples 1, 2 and 3 provided to you.
* Try to filter out relevant information even if the search result is in a different language.

# Example 1
The search result from America Today provides several photographs of the Notre-Dame Cathedral fire on April 15, 2019. <image:i>, <image:j>, <image:k>. None of the images show the Eiffel Tower in the background. 

# Example 2
NONE

# Example 3
The Guardian discusses a report blaming the Syrian government for a toxic gas attack and condemning their use of chemical weapons. The Guardian mentions the Chemical Weapons Convention and the responsibilities of Syria under the convention. According to The Guardian, The White House condemned the Assad regime for defying the norm against chemical weapons use.

# Record
## Claim
Claim: "<image:24> This image shows American mercenaries participating in Ukraine's incursion into Russia's Kursk Oblast in August 2024."

## Actions
```
web_search("American mercenaries Ukraine Kursk Oblast August 2024")
```

# Instructions
In order to find evidence that helps your fact-check, you just ran a web search which yielded a Search Result. **Your task right now is to summarize the Search Result.** What to include:
* information that might be useful for the fact-check (see Record)
* relevant images (refer to images by inserting their reference <image:k>)
* if available: the release date as well as the author or the publisher (e.g. the media company) of the search result.

Do NOT include:
* advertisements
* any other information not related to the Record or the Claim

Additional rules:
* Do not add any additional information besides the information in the Search Result.
* If the Search Result doesn't contain any relevant information for the fact-checking work, simply print one word in capital letters: "NONE".
* Keep your writing style like in the Examples 1, 2 and 3 provided to you.
* Try to filter out relevant information even if the search result is in a different language.

# Example 1
The search result from America Today provides several photographs of the Notre-Dame Cathedral fire on April 15, 2019. <image:i>, <image:j>, <image:k>. None of the images show the Eiffel Tower in the background. 

# Example 2
NONE

The Guardian mentions the Chemical Weapons Convention and the responsibilities of Syria under the convention. According to The Guardian, The White House condemned the Assad regime for defying the norm against chemical weapons use.

¬†—Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ –ú–∏–Ω–æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—ã –æ—Ç 10 —Å–µ–Ω—Ç—è–±—Ä—è –Ω–µ –±—ã–ª–æ —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω–æ –Ω–∏ —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞ –æ–± –æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–º–∏ –≤–æ–π—Å–∫–∞–º–∏ –≥–æ—Ä–æ–¥–∞—Ö. –ü–æ–∑–∂–µ –ú–∏–Ω–æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—ã¬†[–æ–±—ä—è—Å–Ω–∏–ª–æ](https://t.me/mod_russia/19719)
¬†–æ—Ç—Å—Ç—É–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏—Ö –≤–æ–π—Å–∫ ¬´–æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–µ–π –ø–æ —Å–≤–µ—Ä—Ç—ã–≤–∞–Ω–∏—é –∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–±—Ä–æ—Å–∫–µ –ò–∑—é–º—Å–∫–æ-–ë–∞–ª–∞–∫–ª–µ–π—Å–∫–æ–π –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∏¬ª –¥–ª—è –Ω–∞—Ä–∞—â–∏–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è —É—Å–∏–ª–∏–π –ø–æ ¬´–æ—Å–≤–æ–±–æ–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏—é –î–æ–Ω–±–∞—Å—Å–∞¬ª.

¬´–°–µ–π—á–∞—Å –º—ã –≤–∏–¥–∏–º, –∫–∞–∫ —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–µ –≤–æ–π—Å–∫–∞ –±–µ–≥—É—Ç, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –º–æ–≥—É—Ç –¥–µ—Ä–∂–∞—Ç—å –æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—É¬ª, ‚Äî –æ–ø–∏—Å—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥—è—â–µ–µ —É–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–∏–π –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç –ê–ª–µ–∫—Å–∞–Ω–¥—Ä –ö–æ–≤–∞–ª–µ–Ω–∫–æ. –≠—Ç–æ–º—É –ø—Ä–µ–¥—à–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ–≤–∞–ª –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π –∫—Ä—É–ø–Ω—ã–π —É—Å–ø–µ—Ö –í–°–£ –≤ –•–∞—Ä—å–∫–æ–≤—Å–∫–æ–π –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏ ‚Äî –æ—Å–≤–æ–±–æ–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ 8 —Å–µ–Ω—Ç—è–±—Ä—è –≥–æ—Ä–æ–¥–∞ –ë–∞–ª–∞–∫–ª–µ—è, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –±—ã–ª –æ–∫–∫—É–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω —Å –º–∞—Ä—Ç–∞. ¬´–≠—Ç–æ –º–µ—Å—Ç–æ, –≥–¥–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Ç–æ—á–µ–Ω—ã —Å–∫–ª–∞–¥—ã —Å –±–æ–µ–ø—Ä–∏–ø–∞—Å–∞–º–∏ –¥–ª—è –∞—Ä—Ç–∏–ª–ª–µ—Ä–∏–∏, –ø–æ—ç—Ç–æ–º—É \[–µ–µ –æ—Å–≤–æ–±–æ–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ\] –¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ —Å–µ—Ä—å–µ–∑–Ω–æ —É—Å–∏–ª–∏—Ç –æ–≥–Ω–µ–≤—ã–µ –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –í–°–£¬ª, ‚Äî –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç.

–ò–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –æ—Å–≤–æ–±–æ–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ë–∞–ª–∞–∫–ª–µ–∏ –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª–∏–ª–æ –í–°–£ –ª–∏—à–∏—Ç—å —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫—É—é –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫—É, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è —Ç–∞–º —Å–∫–æ–Ω—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∞, –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –¥–µ—Ä–∂–∞—Ç—å –æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—É, –ø–æ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫—É –æ—Ç—Ä–µ–∑–∞–ª–æ –∏—Ö –æ—Ç ¬´–ª–æ–≥–∏—Å—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–π –∞—Ä—Ç–µ—Ä–∏–∏¬ª –í–æ–ª—á–∞–Ω—Å–∫-–ë–æ–ª—å—à–æ–π –ë—É—Ä–ª—É–∫-–ö—É–ø—è–Ω—Å–∫-–ò–∑—é–º, –ø–æ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–π –ø—Ä–æ–∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–∏–ª–æ —Å–Ω–∞–±–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∞—Ä–º–∏–∏, –æ–±—ä—è—Å–Ω—è–µ—Ç —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç. ¬´–ë–µ–∑ —Å–Ω–∞–±–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –≤—Å—è —ç—Ç–∞ –º–∞—Å—Å–∞ –ª–∏—á–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∞ –∏ —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–∏–∫–∏, —Å–∫–æ–Ω—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–∞—è –Ω–∞ –ò–∑—é–º—Å–∫–æ–º –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏, –æ–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–∞—Å—å –±—ã –Ω–µ –±–æ–µ—Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ–π¬ª, ‚Äî –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç –ö–æ–≤–∞–ª–µ–Ω–∫–æ.

–ü–æ —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞–º —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç–∞ –Æ—Ä–∏—è –§–µ–¥–æ—Ä–æ–≤–∞, —É —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏—Ö –≤–æ–π—Å–∫ –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ–º –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏ ¬´–æ—á–µ–Ω—å –∫—Ä—É–ø–Ω—ã–µ –ø–æ—Ç–µ—Ä–∏¬ª: –Ω–µ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —É–±–∏—Ç—ã–º–∏, –Ω–æ –∏ –ø–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏: ¬´–∫–∞–∫ –º–∏–Ω–∏–º—É–º —Å–æ—Ç–Ω–∏ –ø–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö, –µ—Å–ª–∏ –Ω–µ –ø–∞—Ä–∞ —Ç—ã—Å—è—á¬ª.

–í–µ—Ä–æ—è—Ç–Ω–æ–µ –±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–µ –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –ø–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –ø–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–∞—é—Ç –∏ –¥–≤–æ–µ –±—ã–≤—à–∏—Ö –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å–ª—É–∂–∞—â–∏—Ö —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–π –∞—Ä–º–∏–∏. ¬´–ü—Ä–∏ —Å–ø–æ–Ω—Ç–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–º –æ—Ç—Å—Ç—É–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –æ—Å–æ–±–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –ø–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö. –°–≤—è–∑–∏ –≤–Ω—É—Ç—Ä–∏ –ø–æ–¥—Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π –Ω–µ—Ç. –ö—Ç–æ –≥–¥–µ –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è, –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–∏—Ä—ã –Ω–µ –≤—Å–µ–≥–¥–∞ –∑–Ω–∞—é—Ç. –°–æ–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ, –æ–± –æ—Ç—Å—Ç—É–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –Ω–µ –≤—Å–µ –º–æ–≥—É—Ç –∑–Ω–∞—Ç—å¬ª, ‚Äî –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä—è—Ç –æ–Ω–∏. –ë—ã–≤—à–∏–π –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å–ª—É–∂–∞—â–∏–π –æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∏–∑ —ç–ª–∏—Ç–Ω—ã—Ö –ø–æ–¥—Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π –≤ —Ä–∞–∑–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–µ —Å ¬´–í–∞–∂–Ω—ã–º–∏ –∏—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è–º–∏¬ª –æ—Ç–º–µ—Ç–∏–ª, —á—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –•–∞—Ä—å–∫–æ–≤—Å–∫–æ–º –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –æ–±–µ —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—ã –Ω–µ—Å—É—Ç –æ—â—É—Ç–∏–º—ã–µ –ø–æ—Ç–µ—Ä–∏. ¬´–ö–æ–≥–¥–∞ –º–æ–∏ –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä—è—Ç: ‚Äû–ë–ª—è, —Ç–∞–º –ø–∏–∑–¥–µ—Ü‚Äú, –∑–Ω–∞—á–∏—Ç, —á—Ç–æ –≤—Å—ë –ø–ª–æ—Ö–æ¬ª, ‚Äî –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏–ª —Å–æ–±–µ—Å–µ–¥–Ω–∏–∫ ¬´–í–∞–∂–Ω—ã—Ö –∏—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–π¬ª.

### **–ü–æ—á–µ–º—É –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª–∏–ª–∞—Å—å —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∞—è –æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–∞**

–ù–µ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä—è –Ω–∞ —Ç–æ, —á—Ç–æ –≤ –•–∞—Ä—å–∫–æ–≤—Å–∫–æ–π –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏ –±—ã–ª–æ —Å–∫–æ–Ω—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏—Ö –≤–æ–π—Å–∫, —á–µ–º –∑–∞–¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ —Å–∏–ª –í–°–£ –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ–º —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–∫–µ, –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è –±—ã–ª–∞ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∞ –Ω–∞ –æ—Å–æ–±–æ —É—è–∑–≤–∏–º—ã–µ –º–µ—Å—Ç–∞, –≥–¥–µ –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏—Ö –ø–æ–¥—Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π –ø–æ –æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–µ –±—ã–ª–∏ –∏—Å—Ç–æ—â–µ–Ω—ã, –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç —É–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–∏–π –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç –ê–ª–µ–∫—Å–∞–Ω–¥—Ä –ö–æ–≤–∞–ª–µ–Ω–∫–æ. ¬´–†–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–µ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –∑–Ω–∞–ª–æ, —á—Ç–æ —É –Ω–∏—Ö –µ—Å—Ç—å —É—è–∑–≤–∏–º—ã–µ –º–µ—Å—Ç–∞ –≤ –•–∞—Ä—å–∫–æ–≤—Å–∫–æ–π –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏, –æ–Ω–∏ –¥–∞–∂–µ –ø—ã—Ç–∞–ª–∏—Å—å –∏—Ö –≤ –∑–Ω–∞—á–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–π —Å—Ç–µ–ø–µ–Ω–∏ —É—Å–∏–ª–∏—Ç—å. –ó–Ω–∞–ª–∏, –Ω–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Ç–≤—Ä–∞—Ç–∏—Ç—å \[–∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥ —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏–π\] –Ω–µ –º–æ–≥–ª–∏: –Ω–µ—Ö–≤–∞—Ç–∫–∞ —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–æ–≤ —É–∂–µ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ —Å–∫–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –Ω–∞ –∏—Ö –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—è—Ö –ø–æ –≤–µ–¥–µ–Ω–∏—é –æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—ã. –ò —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å –º—ã –Ω–∞–±–ª—é–¥–∞–µ–º –∫–∞—Å–∫–∞–¥–Ω—ã–π –æ–±–≤–∞–ª –æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—ã¬ª, ‚Äî –æ–±—ä—è—Å–Ω—è–µ—Ç –ê–ª–µ–∫—Å–∞–Ω–¥—Ä –ö–æ–≤–∞–ª–µ–Ω–∫–æ.

*   [–ó–°–£ –≤–∂–µ –Ω–∞ –æ–∫–æ–ª–∏—Ü—è—Ö –æ–∫—É–ø–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ–≥–æ –ö—É–ø‚Äô—è–Ω—Å—å–∫–∞](https://cripo.com.ua/news/war/zsu-vzhe-na-okolytsyah-okupovanogo-kup-yanska/ "Permalink to –ó–°–£ –≤–∂–µ –Ω–∞ –æ–∫–æ–ª–∏—Ü—è—Ö –æ–∫—É–ø–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ–≥–æ –ö—É–ø‚Äô—è–Ω—Å—å–∫–∞")
    

–†–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–π –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç –Æ—Ä–∏–π –§–µ–¥–æ—Ä–æ–≤ –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç, —á—Ç–æ –≤ –•–∞—Ä—å–∫–æ–≤—Å–∫–æ–π –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏ —É–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–∞—è –∞—Ä–º–∏—è –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–ª–∞ –Ω–æ–≤—É—é —Ç–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫—É, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è –∏ –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–∏–ª–∞ —É—Å–ø–µ—Ö –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ–º –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏. ¬´–í–°–£ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—Ç –æ—á–µ–Ω—å –¥–∏–Ω–∞–º–∏—á–Ω–æ –∏ —Ñ–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –Ω–µ –∑–∞–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–≤–∞—é—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞ —Ç–æ, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã —à—Ç—É—Ä–º–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å —Ç–µ –∏–ª–∏ –∏–Ω—ã–µ –≥–æ—Ä–æ–¥–∞. –û–Ω–∏ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –∏—Ö –æ–±—Ö–æ–¥—è—Ç, –±–µ—Ä—É—Ç –≤ –∫–æ–ª—å—Ü–æ, –∏ —Ç–æ–≥–¥–∞ –≥–∞—Ä–Ω–∏–∑–æ–Ω—ã —ç—Ç–∏—Ö –≥–æ—Ä–æ–¥–∫–æ–≤ –∏ –Ω–µ–±–æ–ª—å—à–∏—Ö —Å–µ–ª –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –≤—ã–Ω—É–∂–¥–µ–Ω—ã –∫–∞–ø–∏—Ç—É–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å, ‚Äî —Ä–∞—Å—Å–∫–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–π –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç –Æ—Ä–∏–π –§–µ–¥–æ—Ä–æ–≤.

‚Äî –°–µ–π—á–∞—Å —É–∂–µ –ø—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –≤–∑—è—Ç –ö—É–ø—è–Ω—Å–∫, –ø–æ –∫—Ä–∞–π–Ω–µ–π –º–µ—Ä–µ, —Ç–∞ —á–∞—Å—Ç—å, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–æ–º –±–µ—Ä–µ–≥—É. –°–¥–∞–Ω –ò–∑—é–º –∏–ª–∏ –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è –≤ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–µ. –†–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–µ –≤–æ–π—Å–∫–∞ —É—Ö–æ–¥—è—Ç –æ—Ç—Ç—É–¥–∞, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –Ω–µ –ø–æ–ø–∞—Å—Ç—å –≤ –æ–∫—Ä—É–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ. –≠—Ç–æ, –≤ –æ–±—â–µ–º, —Ä–∞–∑—É–º–Ω–æ–µ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ –∫–æ–º–º—É–Ω–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Ä–µ–∑–∞–Ω—ã. –°–∞–º –ø–æ —Å–µ–±–µ –ò–∑—é–º –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞ —Å—Ç—ã–∫–µ –¥–≤—É—Ö —Ä–µ–∫: –û—Å–∫–æ–ª –∏ –°–µ–≤–µ—Ä—Å–∫–∏–π –î–æ–Ω–µ—Ü. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –µ–≥–æ –æ–∫—Ä—É–∂–∏—Ç—å, —Å–∫–∞–∂–µ–º, —Å —Å–µ–≤–µ—Ä–æ-–≤–æ—Å—Ç–æ–∫–∞ –∏–ª–∏ —Å —Å–µ–≤–µ—Ä–∞, —Ç–æ –æ–Ω –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –æ—Ç—Ä–µ–∑–∞–Ω –æ—Ç –ø–æ–¥–≤–æ–∑–∞ –±–æ–µ–ø—Ä–∏–ø–∞—Å–æ–≤ –∏ –≤—Å–µ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–æ—á–µ–≥–æ, –∏ \[—Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∞—è –∞—Ä–º–∏—è\] –≤—ã–Ω—É–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∞ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –∫–∞–ø–∏—Ç—É–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å. –ß—Ç–æ–±—ã —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –Ω–µ —Å–ª—É—á–∏–ª–æ—Å—å, –æ–Ω–∏ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –≤—ã–≤–æ–¥—è—Ç –≤–æ–π—Å–∫–∞, –ø–æ–∫–∞ –µ—Å—Ç—å –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å¬ª.

–Æ—Ä–∏–π –§–µ–¥–æ—Ä–æ–≤ —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞–µ—Ç, —á—Ç–æ –í–°–£ —Ç–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –∏ –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–∏–≥—Ä–∞–ª–∏ —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–µ –≤–æ–π—Å–∫–∞, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–º –Ω–µ —Ö–≤–∞—Ç–∏–ª–æ —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–æ–≤ –¥–ª—è —Å–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è. ¬´\[–°–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞\] –±—ã–ª–∞ –ø—Ä–æ—Ä–≤–∞–Ω–∞ –æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–∞ –≤ —Ä–∞–π–æ–Ω–µ –ë–∞–ª–∞–∫–ª–µ–∏. –ê –∑–∞—Ç–µ–º —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–µ –≤–æ–π—Å–∫–∞ –±—ã–ª–∏ —Ä–∞–∑–±—Ä–æ—Å–∞–Ω—ã –≥–∞—Ä–Ω–∏–∑–æ–Ω–∞–º–∏ –ø–æ —Ä–∞–∑–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã–º –≥–æ—Ä–æ–¥–∫–∞–º, —Å–µ–ª–∞–º. –≠—Ç–∏ –≥–∞—Ä–Ω–∏–∑–æ–Ω—ã —á–∞—Å—Ç–æ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–ª–∏ –∏–∑ –†–æ—Å–≥–≤–∞—Ä–¥–∏–∏, –∞ —Ç–∞–∫–∂–µ –º–æ–±–∏–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –∏–∑ —Ç–∞–∫ –Ω–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞–µ–º—ã—Ö –Ω–∞—Ä–æ–¥–Ω—ã—Ö —Ä–µ—Å–ø—É–±–ª–∏–∫.

–†–æ—Å–≥–≤–∞—Ä–¥–∏—è –≤ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—Ü–∏–ø–µ –≤–æ–µ–≤–∞—Ç—å –Ω–µ —É–º–µ–µ—Ç, –æ–Ω–∞ –Ω–µ –¥–ª—è —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–Ω–∞–∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∞. –ó–∞–¥–∞—á–∞ —ç—Ç–∏—Ö –≥–∞—Ä–Ω–∏–∑–æ–Ω–æ–≤ –∏ –≥–≤–∞—Ä–¥–µ–π—Å–∫–∏—Ö –ø–æ–ª–∫–æ–≤ –∑–∞–∫–ª—é—á–∞–ª–∞—Å—å –≤ —Ç–æ–º, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –¥–µ—Ä–∂–∞—Ç—å –≤ –ø–æ–¥—á–∏–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –º–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ–µ –Ω–∞—Å–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ. –ê —Å—Ä–µ–¥–∏ –º–æ–±–∏–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –º–Ω–æ–≥–∏–µ –≤ –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π —Ä–∞–∑ –≤–∑—è–ª–∏ –≤ —Ä—É–∫–∏ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç, –Ω–∞–¥–µ–ª–∏ –∫–∞—Å–∫—É, –º–æ—Ç–∏–≤–∞—Ü–∏–∏ \[—É –Ω–∏—Ö –Ω–µ—Ç\] –Ω–∏–∫–∞–∫–æ–π. –†–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–µ —Ä–µ–≥—É–ª—è—Ä–Ω—ã–µ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏ –±—ã–ª–∏ –æ—Ç–≤–µ–¥–µ–Ω—ã —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–æ–±–µ—Ä–µ–∂—å–µ –≤ –•–µ—Ä—Å–æ–Ω—Å–∫—É—é –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç—å, —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ –î–æ–Ω–µ—Ü–∫–æ–µ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –≥–¥–µ –æ–Ω–∏ –ø—ã—Ç–∞–ª–∏—Å—å —à—Ç—É—Ä–º–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø—Ä–∏–≥–æ—Ä–æ–¥ –î–æ–Ω–µ—Ü–∫–∞, –∑–∞–Ω—è—Ç—ã–π –í–°–£. –ü–æ—ç—Ç–æ–º—É –≤–æ—Ç —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π —Ä–∞–∑–≥—Ä–æ–º¬ª, ‚Äî –æ–±—ä—è—Å–Ω—è–µ—Ç –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç.

–≠—Ç–æ –∂–µ –ø–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–∞–µ—Ç –≤ —Ä–∞–∑–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–µ —Å ¬´–í–∞–∂–Ω—ã–º–∏ –∏—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è–º–∏¬ª –∏ —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–π –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å–ª—É–∂–∞—â–∏–π, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –±—ã–ª –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ–º –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏. ¬´\[–ü–æ–¥–≤–µ–¥–æ–º—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ\] –ú–∏–Ω–æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—ã \[–≤–æ–π—Å–∫–∞\], –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∞ –í–æ—Å—Ç–æ–∫, –≤—ã—à–ª–∏ —Å —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –µ—â–µ –≤ –∏—é–ª–µ –≤ –ë–µ–ª–≥–æ—Ä–æ–¥—Å–∫—É—é –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç—å. –ù–∞ —Ç–æ—Ç –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç –≤ –ò–∑—é–º–µ —è –≤—Å—Ç—Ä–µ—á–∞–ª –ë–ê–†–°–æ–≤ (_–±–æ–µ–≤–æ–π –∞—Ä–º–µ–π—Å–∫–∏–π —Ä–µ–∑–µ—Ä–≤ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—ã_¬†‚Äî¬†**–ü—Ä–∏–º. —Ä–µ–¥.**), –æ–ø–æ–ª—á–µ–Ω—Ü–µ–≤ –∏ –≤–æ–π—Å–∫–∞ –ü–í–û –ó–∞–ø–∞–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ –æ–∫—Ä—É–≥–∞. –ü–æ—Å–ª–µ \[–∏—Ö\] –≤—ã—Ö–æ–¥–∞ –≤ –ò–∑—é–º –∑–∞—à—ë–ª –°–û–ë–† –∏ –û–ú–û–ù. –°–æ–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ, —Ç–∞–º –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–ª–∏—Å—å —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ ‚Äû–ë–ê–†–°–∏–∫–∏‚Äú, –æ–ø–æ–ª—á–µ–Ω—Ü—ã –∏ –†–æ—Å–≥–≤–∞—Ä–¥–∏—è¬ª, ‚Äî –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç –æ–Ω.

–ü–æ —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞–º —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç–∞ –§–µ–¥–æ—Ä–æ–≤–∞, —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–µ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—á–∏—Ç–∞–ª–æ—Å—å –≤ –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–µ —Å–∏—Ç—É–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–±—Ä–æ—Å–∏–ª–æ –±–æ–µ–≤—ã–µ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏ —Å —é–≥–∞ –•–∞—Ä—å–∫–æ–≤—Å–∫–æ–π –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–µ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –¥–æ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è. ¬´–°—á–∏—Ç–∞–ª–æ—Å—å, —á—Ç–æ –≤ —Ä–∞–π–æ–Ω–µ —Ä–∞—Å–ø–æ–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –∏–∑—é–º—Å–∫–æ–π –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∏ –Ω–∏—á–µ–≥–æ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—à–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å–ª—É—á–∏—Ç—å—Å—è –Ω–µ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç. –ü—Ä–æ—Å—á–µ—Ç –∑–∞–∫–ª—é—á–∞–ª—Å—è –≤ —Ç–æ–º, —á—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –±—ã–ª–∞ –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∞ –≤–µ—Ä–æ—è—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —Ç–æ–≥–æ, —á—Ç–æ —É–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–∏–µ –≤–æ–π—Å–∫–∞ –Ω–∞—á–Ω—É—Ç —Ç–∞–º –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ¬ª, ‚Äî –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç –§–µ–¥–æ—Ä–æ–≤.

¬´–†–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–µ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ —Å –ø—Ä–æ—Ñ–µ—Å—Å–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–π —Ç–æ—á–∫–∏ –∑—Ä–µ–Ω–∏—è –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∏–≤–∞—é—Ç –∫–∞–∫ –æ—á–µ–Ω—å —Å–ª–∞–±–æ–µ. –≠—Ç–æ –ª—é–¥–∏, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ —É–º–µ—é—Ç –±—Ä–æ—Å–∞—Ç—å –≤ –±–æ–π –∑–Ω–∞—á–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –∂–∏–≤–æ–π —Å–∏–ª—ã, –Ω–æ –æ—Ç—Å—É—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç –∏–Ω–∏—Ü–∏–∞—Ç–∏–≤–∞ –≤ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –ø—Ä–∏–∫–∞–∑–∞. –ù–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–æ ‚Äû–∑–∞–Ω—è—Ç—å —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π-—Ç–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Å—Ç–æ–∫‚Äú, –∞ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å, –ª—É—á—à–µ –∑–∞–Ω—è—Ç—å –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–π –ø–µ—Ä–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Å—Ç–æ–∫ —Ä—è–¥—ã—à–∫–æ–º, –Ω–æ —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–µ–¥–æ–ø—É—Å—Ç–∏–º–∞—è –≤–µ—â—å, \[—Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ\] —Ç—É–ø–æ–µ —É–ø–æ—Ä–Ω–æ–µ –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø—Ä–∏–∫–∞–∑–∞¬ª, ‚Äî –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –æ–Ω.

¬´–ù–µ–ª—å–∑—è, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –∞—Ä–º–∏—è, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏–ª–∞—Å—å –¥–≤–∞–¥—Ü–∞—Ç—å –ª–µ—Ç, —Å–µ–≥–æ–¥–Ω—è —Ç–∞–∫–∞—è: –≤—Å–µ, –º—ã –±—É–¥–µ–º —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç—å –ø–æ-–¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–º—É. –ù–∞—Å –∑–∞—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è–ª–∏ –±—ã—Ç—å —Ç—É–ø—ã–º–∏ –∏ –Ω–µ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ç—å –Ω–∏–∫–∞–∫–∏—Ö —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–π, ‚Äî –ø–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–∞–µ—Ç –±—ã–≤—à–∏–π –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å–ª—É–∂–∞—â–∏–π —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–π –∞—Ä–º–∏–∏. ‚Äî –ü–æ–ø—Ä–æ–±—É–π —Å–µ—Ä–∂–∞–Ω—Ç—É —Å–∫–∞–∂–∏, —á—Ç–æ —Ç—ã —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞–µ—à—å, —á—Ç–æ –ª—É—á—à–µ –≤–æ—Ç —Ç–∞–∫ –≤–æ—Ç. –¢–µ–±–µ –µ–±–∞–ª–æ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ —Å–ª–æ–º–∞—é—Ç, –µ—Å–ª–∏ –Ω–µ –∑–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–µ–ª—è—Ç —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É. –ò —Ç–∞–∫ –Ω–∞ –≤—Å–µ—Ö —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω—è—Ö. –í–µ—Ä—Ö–æ–≤–Ω—ã–π –≥–ª–∞–≤–Ω–æ–∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥—É—é—â–∏–π –ø—Ä–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ—Ç —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ¬†‚Äû‚Äé–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ‚Äú‚Äé —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è ‚Äî –∞ –≤—Å–µ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω—ã –∏—Ö –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è—Ç—å. –ò –µ—Å–ª–∏ —á—Ç–æ, –æ–Ω–∏ –±—É–¥—É—Ç –Ω–µ—Å—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω–∏–µ, –Ω–µ –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ —Å–≤–µ—Ä—Ö—É –¥–æ–ª–±–æ–µ–±—ã, –∞ –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ¬†‚Äû‚Äé–≤—ã –ø–ª–æ—Ö–æ \[–ø—Ä–∏–∫–∞–∑—ã\] –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è–µ—Ç–µ, –≤—ã –Ω–µ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ‚Äú¬ª‚Äé, ‚Äî –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç –æ–Ω.

¬´–°–∞–º—ã–µ —É—Å–ø–µ—à–Ω—ã–µ –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∑–∞ –≤—Å—é –º–æ—é —Å–ª—É–∂–±—É –±—ã–ª–∏ —Ç–µ, –æ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã—Ö –∑–Ω–∞–ª–∏ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –º—ã. –¢–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Ç–µ –ª—é–¥–∏, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –≤ –Ω–µ–π —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—Ç. –ü–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ —Å—Ç–æ–∏—Ç —Ç–∞–∫–∏–º –∑–∞–Ω—è—Ç—å—Å—è –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—é‚Ä¶ –ü–æ—ç—Ç–æ–º—É –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –º—ã —Å–∞–º–∏ —Ä–µ—à–∞–ª–∏, —á—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å, –Ω–µ –æ–∂–∏–¥–∞—è –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥—ã —Å–≤–µ—Ä—Ö—É –∏–ª–∏ –ø–æ–∫–∞ –∫–∞—á–Ω—É—Ç —Å–≤—è–∑—å, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã —É—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏—Ç—å, —Å–≤—è–∑–∞—Ç—å—Å—è, –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏—Ç—å —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ, —É—Ç–æ—á–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏ –ø—Ä–æ—á—É—é —Ö–µ—Ä–Ω—é, –º—ã –≤—Å–µ–≥–¥–∞ –≤—Å–µ –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è–ª–∏ –Ω–∞ 100 %¬ª, ‚Äî –æ—Ç–º–µ—á–∞–µ—Ç –±—ã–≤—à–∏–π –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å–ª—É–∂–∞—â–∏–π –æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∏–∑ —ç–ª–∏—Ç–Ω—ã—Ö –ø–æ–¥—Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π –í–° –†–§.

–ù–∞–∫–∞–Ω—É–Ω–µ, 9 —Å–µ–Ω—Ç—è–±—Ä—è, –ú–∏–Ω–æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—ã¬†[–ø–æ–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–æ](https://t.me/mod_russia/19710)
¬†–∫–∞–¥—Ä—ã –ø–µ—Ä–µ–±—Ä–æ—Å–∫–∏ –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–∏–∫–∏ –≤ –•–∞—Ä—å–∫–æ–≤—Å–∫—É—é –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç—å, –Ω–æ —ç—Ç–æ –ø–æ–¥–∫—Ä–µ–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–µ –ø–æ–º–æ–≥–ª–æ –æ—Ç—Å—Ç–æ—è—Ç—å –≥–æ—Ä–æ–¥–∞. ¬´–≠—Ç–∏—Ö –ø–æ–¥–∫—Ä–µ–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π –∫—Ä–∞–π–Ω–µ –Ω–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ, ‚Äî –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç –Æ—Ä–∏–π –§–µ–¥–æ—Ä–æ–≤. ‚Äî –î–∞–∂–µ –≤–µ—Ä—Ç–æ–ª–µ—Ç–∞–º–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–±—Ä–∞—Å—ã–≤–∞–ª–∏ –ª–∏—á–Ω—ã–π —Å–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤ –∏ –ª–µ–≥–∫—É—é —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–∏–∫—É. –ù–æ —ç—Ç–æ –≤—Å–µ —Ä–∞–≤–Ω–æ, —á—Ç–æ –ø—ã—Ç–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –∏–∑ –ø–∏–ø–µ—Ç–∫–∏ –Ω–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç—å —Å—Ç–∞–∫–∞–Ω, –ø—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –±–µ—Å—Å–º—ã—Å–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∞¬ª.

–ê–ª–µ–∫—Å–∞–Ω–¥—Ä –ö–æ–≤–∞–ª–µ–Ω–∫–æ –æ–±—ä—è—Å–Ω—è–µ—Ç —ç—Ç–æ —Ç–µ–º, —á—Ç–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–±—Ä–æ—Å–∫–∞ –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–∏ –±—ã–ª–∞ –ª–∏—à—å –ø—Ä–æ–ø–∞–≥–∞–Ω–¥–∏—Å—Ç—Å–∫–∏–º –∂–µ—Å—Ç–æ–º. ¬´–†–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–π –∞—Ä–º–∏–∏ —Å—Ä–æ—á–Ω–æ –ø–æ–Ω–∞–¥–æ–±–∏–ª–æ—Å—å –¥–µ–º–æ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –Ω–µ–∫—É—é –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å, —á—Ç–æ ‚Äû–ø–æ–º–æ—â—å –±–ª–∏–∑–∫–∞‚Äú, ‚Äû–º—ã —Å–≤–æ–∏—Ö –Ω–µ –±—Ä–æ—Å–∞–µ–º‚Äú, —è–∫–æ–±—ã –æ–Ω–∏ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤—ã –æ–∫–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫—É —Ç–µ–º –ø–æ–¥—Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è–º, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –æ–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–∏—Å—å –≤ —Å–ª–æ–∂–Ω–æ–π —Å–∏—Ç—É–∞—Ü–∏–∏. –ù–æ —ç—Ç–∞ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–±—Ä–æ—Å–∫–∞ –∏–º–µ–ª–∞ –Ω–µ–æ—Ä–≥–∞–Ω–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π, —Ö–∞–æ—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–π —Ö–∞—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–µ—Ä, –æ–Ω–∞ –Ω–µ –º–æ–≥–ª–∞ –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–∏—Ç—å –Ω–∏–∫–∞–∫–æ–π –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–∏¬ª, ‚Äî –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç.

–ü–æ –µ–≥–æ —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞–º, —Ç–µ –ø–æ–¥—Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –∑–∞—à–ª–∏ –≤ –∑–æ–Ω—É –±–æ–µ–≤—ã—Ö –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–π –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–∏, –±—ã–ª–∏ –æ–±—Ä–µ—á–µ–Ω—ã. –ú–Ω–æ–≥–∏–µ –∏–∑ –Ω–∏—Ö –¥–∞–≤–Ω—ã–º-–¥–∞–≤–Ω–æ —Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–ª–∏ —Ä–æ—Ç–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∏–ª–∏ –≤—ã–≤–æ–¥–∞ –¥–ª—è –≤–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –±–æ–µ—Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –∏–∑-–∑–∞ –ø–æ–Ω–µ—Å–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –¥–æ —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ —Å–µ—Ä—å–µ–∑–Ω—ã—Ö –ø–æ—Ç–µ—Ä—å. ¬´–í –±–ª–∏–∂–∞–π—à–µ–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –º—ã –±—É–¥–µ–º —É–∑–Ω–∞–≤–∞—Ç—å –æ –±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–º –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ –ø–æ–¥—Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–π –∞—Ä–º–∏–∏, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –ø–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—É –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Å—Ç–∞–ª–∏ —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å, –ø–æ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫—É –≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–æ –≤—ã–≤–æ–¥–∞ –Ω–∞ –≤–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –±–æ–µ—Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –∏—Ö –∫–∏–Ω—É–ª–∏ –≤ —Å–∞–º—É—é –º—è—Å–æ—Ä—É–±–∫—É, —Å–∞–º–æ–µ –∂–µ—Ä–ª–æ –±–æ–µ–≤—ã—Ö —Å—Ç–æ–ª–∫–Ω–æ–≤–µ–Ω–∏–π¬ª, ‚Äî –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç –æ–Ω.

*   [–°–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –¥–ª–∏—Ç—å—Å—è —ç—Ç–∞ –≤–æ–π–Ω–∞ –∏ –∫–∞–∫ –£–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω–µ –≤ –Ω–µ–π –ø–æ–±–µ–¥–∏—Ç—å. –ú–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–≤—É—Ö –≤—ã—Å–æ–∫–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Ñ–µ—Å—Å–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö —É–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–∏—Ö –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞–ª–æ–≤](https://cripo.com.ua/main/skolko-mozhet-dlytsya-eta-vojna-y-kak-ukrayne-v-nej-pobedyt-mnenye-dvuh-vysokoprofessyonalnyh-ukraynskyh-generalov/ "–°–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –¥–ª–∏—Ç—å—Å—è —ç—Ç–∞ –≤–æ–π–Ω–∞ –∏ –∫–∞–∫ –£–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω–µ –≤ –Ω–µ–π –ø–æ–±–µ–¥–∏—Ç—å. –ú–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–≤—É—Ö –≤—ã—Å–æ–∫–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Ñ–µ—Å—Å–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö —É–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–∏—Ö –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞–ª–æ–≤")
    

### **–ß–µ–º —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–π –∞—Ä–º–∏–∏ –≥—Ä–æ–∑–∏—Ç –ø—Ä–æ—Ä—ã–≤ –í–°–£**

–û—Å–≤–æ–±–æ–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ö—É–ø—è–Ω—Å–∫–∞ –∏ –ò–∑—é–º–∞ –≤–∞–∂–Ω–æ –≤ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–º —Å–º—ã—Å–ª–µ —Ç–µ–º, —á—Ç–æ –æ–Ω–æ –æ—Ç—Ä–µ–∑–∞–µ—Ç —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–µ –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∏ –æ—Ç –ø—É—Ç–µ–π —Å–Ω–∞–±–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –∏ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç –í–°–£ –ø—É—Ç—å –Ω–∞ –õ—É–≥–∞–Ω—Å–∫–æ–µ –∏ –î–æ–Ω–µ—Ü–∫–æ–µ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç —É–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–∏–π –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç –ê–ª–µ–∫—Å–∞–Ω–¥—Ä –ö–æ–≤–∞–ª–µ–Ω–∫–æ. ¬´–≠—Ç–∏ –≥–æ—Ä–æ–¥–∞ –≤–∞–∂–Ω—ã —Ç–µ–º, —á—Ç–æ –æ–Ω–∏ —è–≤–ª—è—é—Ç—Å—è –Ω–µ–æ—Ç—ä–µ–º–ª–µ–º–æ–π —á–∞—Å—Ç—å—é –ª–æ–≥–∏—Å—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏—Ö –∞—Ä—Ç–µ—Ä–∏–π –ø–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–æ–∫ —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–∏–∫–∏, –º–∞—Ç–µ—Ä–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ-—Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–µ–Ω–∏—è, –±–æ–µ–ø—Ä–∏–ø–∞—Å–æ–≤, –ª–∏—á–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∞ –∫–∞–∫ –≤ –•–∞—Ä—å–∫–æ–≤—Å–∫—É—é –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç—å, —Ç–∞–∫ –∏ –≤ —Ü–µ–ª–æ–º –Ω–∞ –¥–æ–Ω–±–∞—Å—Å–∫–∏–π –ø–ª–∞—Ü–¥–∞—Ä–º. –ö—É–ø—è–Ω—Å–∫ —è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –æ—á–µ–Ω—å –≤–∞–∂–Ω—ã–º –ª–æ–≥–∏—Å—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–º —É–∑–ª–æ–º, —Å–µ—Ä–¥—Ü–µ–º —ç—Ç–æ–π –∞—Ä—Ç–µ—Ä–∏–∏.

–ß–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –Ω–µ–≥–æ —à–ª–æ –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≥–æ—Ä–æ–¥–∞ –ò–∑—é–º, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π —Å—Ç–∞–ª —Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–æ–º —Å–æ—Å—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Ç–æ—á–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å–∞–º–æ–π –±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–π –±—Ä–æ–Ω–µ—Ç–∞–Ω–∫–æ–≤–æ–π –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø—ã —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏—Ö –æ–∫–∫—É–ø–∞–Ω—Ç–æ–≤ –∑–∞ –≤—Å–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –ø–æ–ª–Ω–æ–º–∞—Å—à—Ç–∞–±–Ω–æ–≥–æ –≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –≤ –£–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—É, ‚Äî –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç. ‚Äî –ò –≤—Å—è —ç—Ç–∞ –º–∞—Å—Å–∞ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–∞ –±—ã–ª–∞ –∏–¥—Ç–∏ –≤ —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—É –°–ª–∞–≤—è–Ω—Å–∫–∞ –∏ –ö—Ä–∞–º–∞—Ç–æ—Ä—Å–∫–∞. –°–µ–π—á–∞—Å –ø–ª–∞–Ω—ã –ø–æ –∑–∞—Ö–≤–∞—Ç—É –°–ª–∞–≤—è–Ω—Å–∫–∞ –∏ –ö—Ä–∞–º–∞—Ç–æ—Ä—Å–∫–∞ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞—Ç—å –∞–Ω–Ω—É–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏. –ü–æ—Ç–µ—Ä—è \[—Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–π –∞—Ä–º–∏–µ–π\] —Ç–∞–∫–∏—Ö –Ω–∞—Å–µ–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –ø—É–Ω–∫—Ç–æ–≤ –∫–∞–∫ –ö—É–ø—è–Ω—Å–∫ –∏ –ò–∑—é–º –ø–æ–ª–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é —Ä—É—à–∏—Ç —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—É –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –¥–æ–Ω–±–∞—Å—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ –ø–ª–∞—Ü–¥–∞—Ä–º–∞ –∏ –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–µ—Ç –í–°–£ –≤ –¥–∞–ª—å–Ω–µ–π—à–µ–º —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∏–≤–∞—Ç—å –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—è —É–∂–µ –Ω–µ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –≤ –•–∞—Ä—å–∫–æ–≤—Å–∫–æ–π –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏, –Ω–æ –∏ –≤ –õ—É–≥–∞–Ω—Å–∫–æ–º –∏ –î–æ–Ω–µ—Ü–∫–æ–º –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è—Ö¬ª.

–í –±–ª–∏–∂–∞–π—à–∏–µ –¥–Ω–∏ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –æ–∂–∏–¥–∞—Ç—å, —á—Ç–æ –•–∞—Ä—å–∫–æ–≤—Å–∫–∞—è –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç—å –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –æ—Å–≤–æ–±–æ–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∞, —É–≤–µ—Ä–µ–Ω —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–π –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç –Æ—Ä–∏–π –§–µ–¥–æ—Ä–æ–≤. ¬´–≠—Ç–æ –Ω–µ —Ä–µ—à–∞—é—â–µ–µ —Å—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –Ω–æ –æ—á–µ–Ω—å –∫—Ä—É–ø–Ω—ã–π —É—Å–ø–µ—Ö –í–°–£¬ª, ‚Äî –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç –æ–Ω. –ü–æ –µ–≥–æ —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞–º, —Ç–æ–≥–¥–∞ –≤–æ–æ—Ä—É–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Å–∏–ª—ã –£–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—ã —Å–º–æ–≥—É—Ç –ø–µ—Ä–µ–±—Ä–æ—Å–∏—Ç—å –∑–Ω–∞—á–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –ª–∏—á–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∞ –∏ –Ω–∞ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–µ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è.

------------------

### **–†–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–π –∞—Ä–º–∏–∏ –Ω–µ —Ö–≤–∞—Ç–∞–µ—Ç —Å–∏–ª –¥–ª—è –æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—ã**

–ï—â–µ –æ–¥–Ω–æ –Ω–µ –º–µ–Ω–µ–µ –≤–∞–∂–Ω–æ–µ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –Ω–∞ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–º –ø—Ä–æ–¥–æ–ª–∂–∞—é—Ç –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞—Ç—å —Å–∏–ª—ã –í–°–£, ‚Äî –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–æ–ª–∏—Ä—É–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–º–∏ –≤–æ–π—Å–∫–∞–º–∏ –ø–ª–∞—Ü–¥–∞—Ä–º –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–æ–º –±–µ—Ä–µ–≥—É –î–Ω–µ–ø—Ä–∞ –≤ –•–µ—Ä—Å–æ–Ω—Å–∫–æ–π –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏. –£–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–æ–µ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–æ—Å—å —Ç–∞–º 29 –∞–≤–≥—É—Å—Ç–∞. –í —Ç–æ—Ç –¥–µ–Ω—å, –ø–æ¬†[–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º](https://www.facebook.com/watch/?v=1018539645523163)
¬†–æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ–π –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∏ –í–°–£ ¬´–ö–∞—Ö–æ–≤–∫–∞¬ª, –µ–π —É–¥–∞–ª–æ—Å—å ¬´–ø—Ä–æ—Ä–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø–µ—Ä–≤—É—é –ª–∏–Ω–∏—é –æ–±–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—ã¬ª –≤ –•–µ—Ä—Å–æ–Ω—Å–∫–æ–π –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏. ¬´109 –ø–æ–ª–∫ ‚Äû–î–ù–†‚Äú –æ—Ç–æ—à–µ–ª —Å–æ —Å–≤–æ–∏—Ö –ø–æ–∑–∏—Ü–∏–π, —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–µ –¥–µ—Å–∞–Ω—Ç–Ω–∏–∫–∏, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –±—ã–ª–∏ –∏—Ö –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–æ–π, —Å–±–µ–∂–∞–ª–∏ —Å –ø–æ–ª—è –±–æ—è¬ª, ‚Äî¬†[–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏–ª–æ—Å—å](https://www.facebook.com/watch/?v=1018539645523163)

¬†—É–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–∏–π —Ñ–ª–∞–≥ –≤ –∫—Ä—É–ø–Ω–æ–º –Ω–∞—Å–µ–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–º –ø—É–Ω–∫—Ç–µ –í—ã—Å–æ–∫–æ–ø–æ–ª—å–µ.

–¢–æ—á–Ω–∞—è —á–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–π –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∏, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–æ–º –±–µ—Ä–µ–≥—É –î–Ω–µ–ø—Ä–∞, –≥–¥–µ –£–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω–∞ –≤–µ–¥–µ—Ç –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –Ω–µ–∏–∑–≤–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–∞. –ü–æ —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã–º –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–∞–º, –Ω–∞ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —Ç–∞–º –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏–ª–æ—Å—å –æ—Ç¬†[20](https://www.currenttime.tv/a/ukraine-russia-war-kherson/31989285.html)

¬†—Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏—Ö –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö. –ù–µ—Ç —Ç–æ—á–Ω—ã—Ö –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –∏ –æ —á–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ —É–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–æ–π –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∏. –ò—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫ ¬´–í–∞–∂–Ω—ã—Ö –∏—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–π¬ª –∏–∑ —á–∏—Å–ª–∞ –±—ã–≤—à–∏—Ö —Å–æ—Ç—Ä—É–¥–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤ —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–π —Å–ø–µ—Ü—Å–ª—É–∂–±—ã, –ø–æ–∂–µ–ª–∞–≤—à–∏–π –æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –∞–Ω–æ–Ω–∏–º–Ω—ã–º, –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç, —á—Ç–æ –¥–ª—è –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –≤ –•–µ—Ä—Å–æ–Ω—Å–∫–æ–π –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏ –£–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª–∞ ¬´–¥–æ–≤–æ–ª—å–Ω–æ —Å–∫—Ä–æ–º–Ω—ã–µ —Ä–µ–∑–µ—Ä–≤—ã¬ª: –∏—Ö —á–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å ‚Äî 10‚Äì12 —Ç—ã—Å—è—á —á–µ–ª–æ–≤–µ–∫.

–û–¥–Ω–∞–∫–æ, –ø–æ –µ–≥–æ —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞–º, —É –£–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—ã –µ—Å—Ç—å –µ—â–µ —Ä–µ–∑–µ—Ä–≤—ã, –Ω–µ –±—Ä–æ—à–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –Ω–µ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω—ã –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª–∏—Ç—å —Ä–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–π —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–µ –∑–∞–º–∫–Ω—É—Ç—å –æ–∫—Ä—É–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≤–æ–∫—Ä—É–≥ –ø—Ä–æ—Ä–≤–∞–≤—à–∏—Ö—Å—è –≤–ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥ –≤–æ–π—Å–∫. –ú–∞–∫—Å–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω—É—é –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∫—É —É–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–∏—Ö —Å–∏–ª –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ–º —Ñ—Ä–æ–Ω—Ç–µ¬†[–ø—Ä–∏–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç](https://www.currenttime.tv/a/rf-boitsya-poteryat-litso-i-poetomu-otdaet-svoih-soldat-na-myaso-na-pravom-beregu-dnepra-eksperty-o-rasklade-sil-na-yuge-ukrainy-/32011763.html)
 —É–∫—Ä–∞–∏–Ω—Å–∫–∏–π –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç –†–æ–º–∞–Ω –°–≤–∏—Ç–∞–Ω: –ø–æ –µ–≥–æ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º, —Ç–∞–º –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è 30 —Ç—ã—Å—è—á –±–æ–π—Ü–æ–≤ –í–°–£.
